# Datasheet**

*[Copyright Â© 2023 Edgecore Networks
Corporation]*

[The EAP101 is an enterprise-grade, concurrent dual-band Wi-Fi 6 indoor
access point.
The]

[EAP101 supports 2x2:2 uplink and downlink MU-MIMO between the AP and
multiple
clients,]

[with up to 1.7 Gbps aggregated data rate. The EAP101 is equipped with a
Bluetooth Low
Energy]

[(BLE) radio and ZigBee, enabling value-added applications such as
iBeacon. The EAP101 can
be]

[operated in a standalone mode or managed by Edgecore's ecCLOUD and
EWS-Series
controllers.]

[In addition, when managed by ecCLOUD, the EAP101 supports AI-enabled
performance]

[detection to help administrators monitor and enhance the network
performance.]

# EAP101**

[INDOOR WI-FI 6 ACCESS
POINT]
